=== Test/Eval/IRIREF_datatype

rdfio.StatementList{
	rdfioutil.Statement{

=== Test/Eval/LITERAL1_ascii_boundaries

rdfio.StatementList{
	rdfioutil.Statement{
		Triple: rdf.Triple{
